RASHIN DACE -  Introduction - Wattpad
Labari ne Wanda zai zo muku da sabon take kan Alhaji Abdulhameed Wanda bai wuce 35yrs ba amma Allah ya bashi rufin Asiri dan za'a iya kiransa Yaro da kudi sai dai matsalar RASHIN DACE mata ba ta farko kazantar ta yasa yayi ta biyu itama kuma ba gwanda da ita da uwar gidan shin zaiyi DACE Kuwa a gaba
Tunda yashigo kwanar area dinsu yake Jin gabansa na faduwa " Hasbunnallah",Abunda Yafada kenan yana dafe kirjinsa area din shiru ne me karancin motoci,G
R
A ne babba gidajen gurin duka sun tsaru wani gida me katafaren gate yayi horn da gudu gate man,Din ya bude mishi Wanda tsoho ne amma ba cancan ba danna hancin motar sa yayi zuwa cikin gidan inda yaje parking space yayi direct,Maimakon ya fito sai ya tsaya yana karema building din kallo gidan sama ne guda uku duka iri daya amma basu manne da juna sam," mtsw" tsaki yayi ya bude kofar yafito dauko suitcase dinshi yayi da suit dinshi,Wanda dukansu black ne dan jan tie dinshi yayi dan yadan saki " sannu da dawowa Alhaji"," yauwa baba ya aiki"Murmushi tsoron yayi " lafiya kalau Alhaji sai dai
" shiru yayi hakan yasa yakalla baban yayi murmushi,Hannunsa ya zura a Aljihu ya ciro kudi batare da ya kirga ba yabashi " ga wannan"
" kai Madallah nagode sosai Alhaji" wani ihu sukaji da alama ta can baya ne da sauri suka nufi bayan,Inda suke Jin hayaniya " na duke ta kiyi wani abu akai"," Rukayya ni kike fadama kinduke ta din ni sa'arkice",Tafada tana nuna ta da hannu ita kuma sai murguda baki take tana hararta " walh Yau Zaki San wa kika taba a gidan nan"" Ina jiranki maijiddah kiyi abunda Zaki iya"" toshikenan" ludayin dake hannunta ta jefa ma Rukayya inda akayi narasa ya sauka kan goshin me gidan nasu," innalillahi Wa'inna illaihir raji'un" baba me gadi Yafada inda su duka suka maida kallonsu zuwa garesu,Yayinda hankulansu ya tashi su duka inda Maijiddah tayi kan yarta da bakinta ke zubar jini,Wacce tun tuni basu bi takanta ba Rukayya kuwa da sauri tadau Yasmin dake kasa Tana kuka yar da bata wuce 1yr ba,Tayi nata part din nan suka bar Abdulhameed tsaye inda shima me gadi ganin yanayin me gidan nasa yasa yakoma gun aikinsa
Tofah su wadan nan wasu irin matane da fada muka fara ganin su harda jini da jifan miji akwai magana a wannan gida gaskiya
tare da Mimsqueen zamu ji komai bayan Sallah in Allah ya kaimu

💕AUTA 💕
*4*
Alhaji usman hakim Abdullahi  shine sunan mahaifinta sananne ne shi a garin dutse, da kano inda yayi aiki har yayi ya retire, dan boko ne kuma mutum mai gaskiya da riqon amana yana da rufin asirin sa dai dai misali maaikacin government ne ta tarayya, yayi aiki ne sunshine gas refinery mallakin gomnatin ta tarayya har yayi retire matar sa daya wata hajiya fatima Al sawy mace mai dattako da sanin ya kamata,mace ce mai kyau da kyaun hali xamu iya cewa asalin kyaun sbd kasancewar ta ruwa biyu mahaifin ta ma ruwa biyun ne mahafiyyar sa baturiya mahaifin sa balarabe ta gurin mahaifiyarta kuma bafulatana kun ga kyan ya samo Asali , amma dai ba fara tas bace itace kalar nan da ake kira wankan tarwada, amma ko turawan ba xasu fada mata kyau ba yayan su 17 tare Allah ya yi wa hudu rasuwa first born
Allah ya kaimu bayan sallah da rai da lfy zamu bi ki kuwa mimsqueen

RASHIN DACE - Chapter 2 - Wattpad
Yana shiga direct part din Maijiddah ya nufa," Salamu Alaikum"" oyoyo dady oyoyo" nan yaran guda biyu suka nufeshi suna tsalle," Ah ikram bakuyi bacci ba why is that" Ya tambayesu na mijin ne yayi saurin karba," dady we are still watching our favorite cartoon""Yes dady akram is right",Cikin muryar su Wanda dukansu ba baki sosai,Kallonsu yayi yana shafasu gwanin sha'awa gimbiyar ko tana gefe ta daura daya kan daya," olright amma yanzu abunda nake so daku kuje ku kwanta haka nan my good children yan Albarka",Basu musa mishi ba sukai mai sallama inda ya dafa kan kowannensu ya musu addu'a,Da gudu sukai hanyar bedroom dinsu suna " momy goodnight"Daga masu hannu tayi batare da tace dasu komai ba,Maida dubansa yayi gunta gaba daya " Maijiddah!"Shiru tayi kamar bata jishi ba sanin halin ta yasa bai maimaita ba inda ya cigaba da abunda ya kawosa," Ina mama"" uhm sai yanzu ka tuna da maman nazata ae ka manta",Tafada tana ciccin kamshi ita a dole Tana fushi," ya bakin nata" shiru tamai " haba magana nake miki"," to tayi bacci sai da nasa aka sayo mata medicine a chemist saboda matarka Yau ta kusa kashe ta"
" uhm Allah ya kyau ta amma ku duka zan dau mataki akanku nan kusa bada jimawa ba zan baku mamaki," badai zaman lafiya bane bakuso kunfiso juyi ta samun bakin ciki to muje zuwa shege ja fasa",Nan yayi fadan karshe ya koma mata nasiha amma Sam ko a jikinta tayi alkawarin,Fasa ma Yasmin yar Rukayya baki Ko wani gun taji Ko inda dadi," to good night"Bata ce mai kala ba ya fito yana mamakin hali irin na Maijiddah Sam bata ji,Part dinshi ya nufa yanzu kam angyara ko ina sai dai ba irin kal din nan ba dan dai anturo a boye dattin,A falo ya tadda ta Tana kallon series dinta na fama," uhmm andawo yawon gantalin da bin mata"," A'uzubillahi haba Rukayya wae ke meyake damun kine"Murguda baki tayi tamaida kallonta kan TV "kai Allah Sarki Kulfi da sikander abun tausayi mtsw",Girgiza kai yayi ya nema gefe can dan nesa da ita ya zauna "malam Abincinka na dinning",Shima bai tanka taba ya dau wayarsa yafara duba instagram dinsa yana kalla ce2,Sai da aka tafi talla ta maida hankalinta kanshi," dadyn Yasmin Ko na zubo maka ne" shima bai amsa mata ba matsowa tayi kusa dashi
" Magana fa nake maka" wani irin wari ne yaji ya ziyarce shi matsawa yayi a hankali," Rabu dani naci"," where did you eat kabarni nayi girki gaskiya bazaiyuba",Cigaba yayi da abunda yake batare da ya kalleta ba inda ta cigaba da jero masa halin nata,Ganin da gaske ransa bace yake yasa ta tashi ta koma kusa dashi gab da gab still wani tsami ne ya mai sallama amma ya daure," nace ba da
"" dan Allah kirabu Dani!"Yafada cikin daga murya ya tashi yayi daki yabarta a falon,Yana shiga dakin ya wuce toilet ji yake gaba daya hankalinshi ya tashi kamar zaiyi amai,A kullum hakan yasa Sam baison kasance wa da Rukayya Sam inba dole ba,Kashe datar yayi ya kwanta bata shigo dakin ba har saida yayi bacci me nisa tashigo,Murmushi tayi ganin sa kwance wani irin sha'awar sa take ji a tattare da ita " zaka ma tashi ne",Tafada tana murmushi ta nufeshi gadan gadan,Kanshi ta hau tafara sha shafa shi Tana kissing dinshi asu kumatunsa kamar a mafarki,Yaji wani irin wari na ziyartashi ya bude idanunsa tunkan ya bude ido ya hankade ta gefe," leave me alone!"
" karki sake kusan tata tunda ke ba zaki koya gyara kanki ba kazamar banza you are smelling damn it",Komawa yayi ya cigaba da baccinsa inda abun ya ma Rukayya ciwo sosai wasu hawaye masu zafi ke fito mata a idanunta,Tana masifar son taga Abdul na kusantarta amma Sam ta rasa meyasa yake wulakanta ta kamar ba mace ba nan tacigaba da sheshekar kuka,Kamar a mafarki yaji sheshekar kukan nata ya bude ido sai kawai ya tsinci kanshi da tausayin ta,Inda yaba Kansa rashin gaskiya a dole bai kyauta mata ba sam," kuka kike Rukayya"Yafada cikin muryarsa me sanyi " kiyi hakuri kiyi shiru bazan Kara ba kinji Ko babyna," ke dince nace ki dunga gyara kanki amma Sam kinkasa fahimta ta please kigyara kinji",Yadda yake mata magana yasa taji wani sonshi nakara ratsa ta " Insha Allahu zangyara",Yaji dadin yadda tamai maganar hakan yasa yace," oya kije kiyi wanka dasu brush kizo" Bata bata lokaci ba jiki na rawa ta dira gadon ta fada toilet mamaki take bashi Tana son kasancewa dashi Ko yaushe amma ta kasa nutsuwa ta dau karatun sam,Haka taje tayi duk abunda yasa ta tadawo inda suka fada cikin wani irin yanayi,Dan Rukayya gwanace a wannan fanin sosai duk yadda zata faranta mishi tasani,Hakan yasa duk kazantarta yake hakuri da ita
" Salamu Alaikum"Ikram Tafada cikin tsamin muryarta cike da jin dadi ya amsa " ah babyn dady kece"," eh dady zamu tafi school yanzu"" Ina akram din"Duba wa tayi ta lelleka ta tabbatar bata ga Rukayya ba saita matsa kusa dashi ta tace," kasan yana tsoron Aunty Rukayya muguwa ce ita da
"," ya isa ikram karna karajin haka itama momyn kuce kinji Ko kifada ma akram dinma kinajina Ko," jeki Allah yayi Albarka yadawo daku lafiya""Ameen" tace Tana zumbura baki tafita abunta," akram! Kallonta yayi ya daga mata kai " uhm" murmushi tayi tajawo hannunshi " nagode daka daina fushi kasan fushinka zai iya mun illoli"Kallonta yayi da mamaki " kamarya zai miki illa"" kasan Allah na fushi duk matar da mijinta ke fushi da ita to tabbas hakan na iya jawo mata bala'i," Abu na biyu fushin ka zai iya tarwatse mun zuciyata yamata illa sosai walh ni kadai nasan ya naji a kwana dayar nan danayi bantare Sakai ga fushinka"Kallonta yayi tare da yin murmushi " Rukayya kenan tabbas kina cikin mata masu ilmin addini" sosai da ibada sai dai nakanyi bakin ciki saboda Sam baki aiki da ilmin ki kan kishi Sam da zakiyi amfani da iliminki na addini tabbas da nafi kowa farin ciki"Sosai jikin Rukayya ya mutu " Insha Allahu daga Yau bazan kuma ba dayar dar Allah"" Allah yasa Yafada"" Ameen luv nayi missing Dinka sosai"Murmushi yayi yana kallonta " really" dan tashi tayi daga kujerar ta ta nufeshi tare da rufe eyes dinta alamun zatai kissing dinshi,Harta kusa kaiwa abunda yafaru tsakanin shi da Baby ne ya fado mishi take ya kauce mataAbunda baitaba mata basaidai ko idan tayi kazantar data saba amma Yau tasan tsab take

Yasmin!!"Nan hafsat ta bude idannunta a hankali dan Sam bataji shigowar su ba Tashi tayi ta gyara dankwalin ta " kibarta mana karki tada ita,Abdul Yafada yana kallonsu " sannu da zuwa aunty Rukayya"" yauwa sannu hafsat ya maijiki sannu da kokari walh nagode sosai hafsat"Murmushi hafsat tayi " kai Aunty bakomai walh jikinta da sauki sosai dan dazu tagama gwarancinta Tana kiran momy" dakyar na lallabata tayi bacci dan su ikram ma sunzo dazu suka bar nan" bata gurin hafsat tayi ta zauna,Surutun hafsat ke bashi mamaki sai dai baisan meyasa yana dan uwanta bata kaunar kulashi baSometimes yakan Ji kamar ta tsaneshi yadda take kallonshi kamar hararshi takeWanda ko hakan ne gun hafsat hararshi take a cewarta ya cika girman kai da iyayi
" Ayya ae dole ta baki wahala"Murmushi hafsat tayi " walh aa saboda Yasmin bata da koke2 irin na yara walh data nemeki na lallabata shikenan saita yi shiru"" To Aku inkin gama surutun dare nayi kizo nakaiki gida tunda tazo"Sunkui dakai tayi dan Sam tama manta yana wajen samDaukar hijab dinta tayi inda sukai sallama da Rukayya shiko tuni ya fice abunsaGanin yadda Rukayya ke kissing Yasmin sosai hafsat ta tausaya mata "tabbas uwa uwace" Tafada a ranta,Fita tayi cikin mota ta tadda shi sallama tayi tashi ga ta zauna,Batare da yace mata komai ba ya fisgi motarWayarshi ce tashiga ringing dagota yayi still baby ce abun sosai yabashi haushi yadda ta addabi rayuwarshi,Danna receiving yayi yasa a speaker "hello"Sheshekan kukan datake yasa yayi saurin cire ta daga handsfree din ya kalla hafsatWacce ta nuna bata San ma meya ke ba " inatuki zan kiraki idan naje gida"Yana dadin hakan ya kashe ita dai hafsat mamaki ne ya kamata tunda ba Rukayya baceBa kuma Maijiddah ba dan Sam cikin su ba wacce zata kirashi a yanzu Tana kuka to waye" Yau momy tazo"Ya katse mata tunanin datake kan wacce takira

DAURIN AUREN ABDULHAMEED DA AMINA (can't miss it)

1045; Abu Dawood, no
1768

Koda yakoma part dinsu Rukayya nata mai karar Saudat bai saurareta ba damuwarsa yadda zata dau batun aurenshi idan tajiKasa sanar mata yayi Sam haka suka kwana ba Wanda yace da dan uwansa komaiHaka suka kwanta duk da Rukayya ranta bace yake takawo mai Kara yaki kulataSai dai zancen da Saudat tayi ya tsaya mata a rai sosai " dadin abun dai yar uwar mu zata shigo muga ta tsiya da shegen kazantar mutum"" me hakan ke nufi anya ba abunda Abdul ke boye mun kuwa" tambayar da tama kanta kenan rashin amsar hakan yasa ta gyara kwanciyarta
Da Asuba Abdul yatashi ba irin tashin da baima Rukayya ta tashi tayi sallah ba amma hakan baisamu ba,Wannan na daga cikin dabi'unta dake sawa yana nesantar ta dan Sam bata da son ibadah Sam rayuwarta kawai take yadda take soTashi yayi yashige toilet din yana tsaki yayi alwala yafita a gate suka hadu da Dady shima zai tafi massalaci inda suka gaggaisa suka tafi tare,Koda suka dawo Abdul bai koma part dinsu ba gun iyayenshi ya zauna suna hira kamar yadda suka saba barin yanzu da suke cikin farin cikin aurenshi da hafsatSaudat da su Asma'u ke hada breakfast dake yau girkin Auntynsu ne tare suke a kitchen suna tayata," gunka shegiyar matar bro Ko dan fitowa tace zata taya mutane bata iya ba sai kwanciya"" A'a Saudat hakan baida kyau kidaina ke macece baikamata inkinga yar uwar Ki mace na hakan kidunga zaginta ko tsanarta ba babu Wanda yafi karfin zama hakan" kedai kawai kimata nasiha inbazaki iyaba kiyi shiru",Sosai zancen Auntynsu ya taba ta hakan yasa bata Kara cewa komai ba suka cigaba da aikinsu,Basu kamalla ba sai kusan 9am suka hada komai a dinning har wanka sunyi dan dama tara suke breakfast kowa ya hallara a dinning amma ba idon Rukayya,Dan Yasmin ma Abdul ya fito da ita tana ta kuka gashi basu Zo da me aikinsu ba dan gidan su can gun momy take turata in zatai tafiyaNan sukai breakfast su duka Banda 'yan uwan Abdul mata dake gidajensu sosai suka Sha hira
Rukayya bata tashi ba sai 11:30am tana bude idonta taga rana jawo wayarta dake gefen bedside tayi ganin lokaci  tayi" wayoo na shiga uku ana can ankasaftani"Tashi tayi ta shige toilet ba zancen sallah wanke fuska tayi kawai tafito tacire rigar bacinta ta dauko wata tasaka,Tafito zuwa part dinsu Ammah zaune Ammah da Aunty suke a falo suna lissafin abubuwan hidima da zasu nema tayi sallama tashigaCike da jin kunya tayi mazauni a kasa " A'a Rukayya kinfito"Aunty tafada dan harararta Amma tayi hakan yasa Rukayya tayi saurin sunkui da kanta kasa" Ina kwana Ammah"Can cikin makogoro Ammah ta amsa mata aunty ce ta amsa cike da fara'a suna cikin gaisawa Ammah ta katse su," inafata kinfada ma Hadiza yau yakamata tazo dan kaf dinsu yakamata ace sun hallara akan lokaci tunda kings gobe za'a fara bikin",Tabe fuska Rukayya tayi aunty kuwa kallonta tayi hakan yasa ta fahimci bata San zancen ba" yanzu yaya nizan shiga kasuwa nida Saudat kan suzo mu fara rage mana wasu abubuwan kar aiki yamana yawa Ko"" eh hakan yayi Allah yabamu Sa'a yasa ayi a Sa'a addu'ar kenan"" biki za'ayine"Rukayya tayi saurin tambaya " eh bakisan da hadin Auren Hafsat da Abdul bane"Gaban Rukayya ne yayi wani mummunar faduwa lokaci guda tafara ganin wani iri-iri " Abdul zaiyi aure"Ta tambaya batare da tasan zancen nata ya fito fili ba sam Aunty bata so yadda Ammah tayi ma Rukayya zancen ba tunda ta fahimci Abdul bai fada mata ba
Tashi Rukayya tayi saboda yanayin da take ji jirine yafara dibarta da sauri Aunty dake kusa tatashi ta taimaka mata ta zauna,Ammah Ko tashi tayi tashige ciki abunta dan abunda Rukayya tayi yau yabata haushi sosaiSai dai bata iya zama ba koda ta shiga cikin haka nan tafito ta tarar aunty tashiga kitchen dan hado mata abunda zataci," Rukayya!"Amma tayi kiran sunan Rukayya da kakkausar murya " nasan yadda nasanar miki da zancen auren mijinki bai kyautu ba kiyi hakuri da hakan kuma inaso kisani bawai Za'ayi auren nan bane dan a kuntata miki," bahaka bane ko kadan bani da wani hard feelings kanki haka 'yan uwana inafata zaki fahimceni sai Abu nagaba a matsayina na mace irinki yana da kyau nasanar miki in kina wasu abubuwa daba dai2 ba dan kin kasance kamar 'ya guna kodan Auren Abdul da kikayi kuma ance "Ciwon 'Ya Mace Na 'Ya Macene" Akwai wasu halayenki wadanda yakamata kigyara bacin su bana ganin kina da wani aibu Sam Ko ba haka bane Auntyn Yara"Aunty data shigo tace " tabbas kuwa Rukayya nikaina najima da sanin wannan Wanda inbaki gyara ba zai iya hanaki zama da mijinki yadda kikeso koda baiyi Aureba Wanda shine " KAZANTA",Shiru Rukayya tayi Jin zantukan su tabbas hakane ita kanta ta tsani kazantar da take dan tafara lura da yana daga cikin matsalarta da mijinta tashi Ammah tayi " bara naje nakira yaran nan naji kimata nasiha"Murmushi Aunty tayi hakan yaba Rukayya mamaki shirin su bayan tunda tazo family din tasan basu jituwa Amma gashi yanzu shiri suke da alama kuma sosai" Rukayya kazanta na hana miji samun nutsuwa tare da mace Sam mudin kika kasance jikinki ba gyara haka ma gidanki zaki ga namiji na yawan fushi dake koda bakiyi masa komai ba wani sa'in ma zai dunga zama dakene kawai kamar dan dole kodan yara hakan baidace ba Ko a addini tsafta daga cikin imani sosai tana da muhimmanci dan haka sai kin gyara zaki ji dadin Aurenki Kinji Ko," Abu nagaba bangaren addini kinada matsala nan ma saikin gyara kiyi kokari kigyara kusancinki da mahaliccinki zakiji dadin rayuwarki sosai Allah yasa mudace ga Abinci kikarya Kar yayi sanyi nizan dan fita"
Haka kawai Rukayya taji jikinta yayi sanyi sosai tabbas duk abunda aka fada hakane dan koda take da kishiya da sanda bata da bawani babanci tsakaninta da Abdul bangaren Jin dadin aure,In hakane insha Allahu zata sauya halinta kuma zata zauna da wacce zai aura lafiya Nan tayita tunanin barin yadda tasan dabi'un hafsat haka kawai taji bakomai zata iya Abunda yakara ba Rukayya mamaki yadda yan uwan Abdul duk Wanda yazo yake kula da ita tabbas suna kaunarta dabi'unta ne abun sauyin Ko momynta tadau niyyar bazata sanar musu da auren ba har a gama isha Allahu,Koda Abdul yadawo yasha mamakin yadda ta tarbeshi kuma da sanin aurenshi sosai yaji dadin hakan ya kuma tausaya mata sosai batun yau yasan Rukayya nada kyan zuciya ba da yadda da kaddarah sai rashin tsaftarta da ibada dake damunsa yayi alkawarin taimaka mata dan samun sauyi
Bangaren Zoya kuwa Anata shirin biki Amma bawani sauyi lamarinsu itada Doctor
